   Guṇakāraṇḍavyūha sūtra	GuNa kAraNxavyUha sUtra
   1. śrītriratna bhajanānuśaṃsāvadānam	1. SrI tri ratna Bajana anuSaMsa avadAnam
   om namaḥ śrīratnatrayāyaḥ namaḥ sarvabuddhabodhisattvebhyaḥ //	om namaH SrI ratnatrayAyaH namaH sarva budDa boDisattveByaH //
   yaṃ śrīghano mahābuddhaḥ sarvalokādhipo jinaḥ /	yam SrIGanaH mahAbudDaH sarva loka aDipaH jinaH /
   taṃ nāthaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā vakṣye lokeśasatkathām //	tam nATam SaraNam gatvA vakzye lokeSa sat kaTAm //
   yā śrī bhagavatī devī sarvadharmādhipeśvarī /	yA SrI BagavatI devI sarva Darma aDipa ISvarI /
   tasyā bhaktiprasādena vakṣyāmi bodhisādhanam //	tasyAH Bakti prasAdena vakzyAmi boDi sADanam //
   yena saṃpālitaṃ sarvaṃ traidhātukamidaṃ jagat /	yena saMpAlitam sarvam trEDAtukam idam jagat /
   tasya lokeśvarasyāhaṃ vakṣye sarvārthasādhanam /	tasya lokeSvarasya aham vakzye sarva arTa sADanam /
   tadyathābhūnmahāsattvo jinaśrīrāja ātmavit /	tat yaTA aBUt mahAsattvaH jina SrI rAjaH Atma vid /
   triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā yatirarhan jinātmajaḥ //	tri ratna SaraNam gatvA yatiH arhan jina AtmajaH //
   ekasmin samaye so 'rhad bodhimaṇḍe jināśrame /	ekasmin samaye saH arhat boDimaNxe jina ASrame /
   bodhicaryāvratam dhṛtvā jagaddhitve samāśrayat //	boDi caryA vratam DRtvA jagat hitve samASrayat //
   tadā tatra mahābhijño jayaśrīryatirātmavit /	tadA tatra mahA aBijQaH jaya SrIH yatiH Atma vid /
   saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ sabhāsane samāśrayat //	sadDarmam samupAdezwum saBA Asane samASrayat //
   taṃ dṛṣṭvā śrāvakāḥ sarve bhikṣavo brahmacāriṇaḥ /	tam dRzwvA SrAvakAH sarve BikzavaH brahmacAriNaH /
   tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātumupetya samupāśrayan //	tad sadDarma amRtam pAtum upetya samupASrayan //
   tathānye bodhisattvāśca saṃbodhivratasādhinaḥ /	taTA anye boDisattvAH ca saMboDi vrata sADinaH /
   subhāṣitāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tatsabhāṃ samupāśrayan //	su BAzita amRtam pAtum tad saBAm samupASrayan //
   bhikṣuṇyaścelakāścaivamupāsakā upāsikāḥ /	BikzuNyaH celakAH ca evam upAsakAH upAsikAH /
   vratino 'pi mahāsattvāḥ sambuddhabhakticārikāḥ //	vratinaH api mahAsattvAH sambudDa Bakti cArikAH //
   (Gkv 2)	(Gku 2)
   brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāścāpi rājāno mantriṇo janāḥ /	brAhmaNAH kzatriyAH ca api rAjAnaH mantriNaH janAH /
   amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaḥ paurāḥ sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ //	amAtyAH SrezWinaH pOrAH sArTavAhAH mahA janAH //
   tathā jānapadā grāmyāḥ pārvatikāśca nairgamāḥ /	taTA jAnapadAH grAmyAH pArvatikAH ca nErgamAH /
   tathānye daiśikā lokāḥ saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ //	taTA anye dESikAH lokAH sat Darma guNavAMCinaH //
   sarve te samupāgatya tamarhantaṃ jayaśriyam /	sarve te samupAgatya tam arhantam jaya Sriyam /
   yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya praṇatvā samupāśritāḥ //	yaTAkramam samaByarcya praNatvA samupASritAH //
   tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ kṛtāṃjalipuṭā mudā /	tad sadDarma amRtam pAtum kRta aMjali puwAH mudA /
   śāstāraṃ taṃ samālokya parivṛtya niṣedire //	SAstAram tam samAlokya parivRtya nizedire //
   tadā so 'rhanmahāsattvo bodhisattvo jinātmajaḥ /	tadA saH arhan mahAsattvaH boDisattvaH jina AtmajaH /
   jinaśrīrājannālokya sarvāṃllokān sabhāśrītān //	jina SrI rAjan= Alokya sarvAn= lokAn saBA SrItAn //
   triratnaguṇamāhātmyaṃ śrotuṃ samabhilāṣiṇaḥ /	tri ratna guNa mAhAtmyam Srotum samaBilAziNaH /
   samutthāyāsanāttasya jayaśriyaḥ puro 'grataḥ //	samutTAya AsanAt tasya jaya SriyaH puras agratas //
   udvahannuttarāsaṃgaṃ jānubhūmitalāśritaḥ /	udvahan= uttarAsaMgam jAnu BUmi tala ASritaH /
   pādābjaṃ sāṃjalirnatvā prārthayadevamādarāt //	pAda abjam sAMjaliH natvA prArTayat evam AdarAt //
   bhadanta śrotumichāmi triratnotpattisatkathām /	Badanta Srotum iCAmi tri ratna utpatti sat kaTAm /
   tadbhagavān samupādiśya sambodhayatu māṃ guro //	tad BagavAn samupAdiSya samboDayatu mAm guro //
   iti saṃprārthite tena jinaśrīguṇasaṃbhṛtā /	iti saMprArTite tena jina SrI guNa saMBRtA /
   jayaśrīḥ sumatiḥ śāstā sabhā vīkṣyaivamādiśat //	jaya SrIH sumatiH SAstA saBA vIkzya evam AdiSat //
   sādhu śṛṇu samādhāya jinaśrīrāja sanmate /	sADu SRNu samADAya jina SrI rAja sanmate /
   triratnasya samutpattisatkathāguṇavistaram //	tri ratnasya samutpatti sat kaTA guNa vistaram //
   yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ jinakalpena yoginā /	yaTA me guruNA Adizwam jina kalpena yoginA /
   upaguptena lokānāṃ hitārthe vakṣyate mayā //	upaguptena lokAnAm hita arTe vakzyate mayA //
   tadyathābhūnmahārājaścakravartīṃ narādhipaḥ /	tat yaTA aBUt mahA rAjaH cakravartIm narADipaH /
   aśoko nāma rājendraḥ sarvalokahitārthabhṛt //	aSokaH nAma rAja indraH sarva loka hita arTa BRt //
   ekadā sa mahārājaḥ saddharmaguṇalālasaḥ /	ekadA sa mahA rAjaH sat Darma guNa lAlasaH /
   triratnaguṇamāhātmyaṃ śrotumaicchajjagaddhite //	tri ratna guNa mAhAtmyam Srotum EcCat jagat hite //
   tataḥ sa bhūpatī rājā samantrijanapaurikaḥ /	tatas sa BUpatiH rAjA sa mantri jana pOrikaH /
   pūjopahāramādāya sa saṃvādya mahotsavaiḥ //	pUjA upahAram AdAya sa saMvAdya mahA utsavEH //
   (Gkv 3)	(Gku 3)
   vihāre kukkuṭārāme prayayau saṃpramoditaḥ /	vihAre kukkuwa ArAme prayayO saMpramoditaH /
   tataḥ prāptaḥ sa rājendra praviśya saṃprasāditaḥ //	tatas prAptaH sa rAja indra praviSya saMprasAditaH //
   upaguptaṃ mahābhijñaṃ saṃdadarśa sasāṃghikam /	upaguptam mahA aBijQam saMdadarSa sa sAMGikam /
   tamarhantaṃ samālokya natvā sa sāṃjalirmudā //	tam arhantam samAlokya natvA sa sAMjaliH mudA //
   sahasā samupāgatya yathāvidhi samarcayet /	sahasA samupAgatya yaTAviDi samarcayet /
   tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā pravatvā caraṇāmbuje //	tatas pradakziNIkRtvA pravatvA caraNa ambuje //
   sāṃjalistasya saddharma śrotuṃ puraḥ samāśrayat /	sAMjaliH tasya sadDarma Srotum puras samASrayat /
   tataḥ sarve 'pi logakāśca yathākramamupāgatāḥ //	tatas sarve api logakAH ca yaTAkramam upAgatAH //
   tamarhantaṃ yatiṃ natvā parivṛtya samāśrayan /	tam arhantam yatim natvA parivRtya samASrayan /
   tadāśokaḥ sa rājendro dṛṣṭvā sabhāśritān janān //	tadA aSokaH sa rAja indraH dRzwvA saBA ASritAn janAn //
   utthāya svāsanācchāstuḥ purataḥ samupāśritaḥ /	utTAya svAsanAt SAstuH puratas samupASritaH /
   udvahannuttarāsaṃgaṃ jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ //	udvahan= uttarAsaMgam jAnuByAm Buvi saMsTitaH //
   sāṃjalistaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayedevamādarāt /	sAMjaliH tam yatim natvA prArTayet evam AdarAt /
   bhadanta śrotumichāmi triratnotpattisatkathām //	Badanta Srotum iCAmi tri ratna utpatti sat kaTAm //
   kiṃ triratnamiti khyātam tatsamādeṣṭumarhasi /	kim tri ratnam iti KyAtam tad samAdezwum arhasi /
   iti saṃprārthite rājñā so 'rhan jinātmajaḥ sudhīḥ //	iti saMprArTite rAjQA saH arhan jina AtmajaH suDIH //
   upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivamādiśat //	upaguptaH narendram tam samAlokya evam AdiSat //
   sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja samādhāya jagaddhite //	sADu SRNu mahA rAja samADAya jagat hite //
   yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā te vakṣyate mayā /	yaTA me guruNA Adizwam taTA te vakzyate mayA /
   tadyathādisamudbhūto dharmadhātusvarupakaḥ //	tat yaTA Adi samudBUtaH DarmaDAtu svarupakaH //
   paṃcabuddhāṃśasaṃjāto jagadīśastathāgataḥ /	paMca budDa aMSa saMjAtaH jagadISaH taTAgataH /
   mahābuddho jagannātho jagacchāstā maheśvaraḥ //	mahAbudDaH jagannATaH jagat SAstAH maheSvaraH //
   dharmarājo munīndro 'rhanvairocanasamādhidhṛk /	DarmarAjaH muni indraH arhan vErocana samADi DRk /
   sarvajñaḥ sadguṇādhāraḥ sarvavidyādhipo jinaḥ //	sarvajQaH sat guNa ADAraH sarva vidyA aDipaH jinaH //
   samantabhadrarupāṃgaḥ sugataḥ śrīsukhākaraḥ /	samantaBadra rupa aMgaH sugataH SrI suKa AkaraH /
   ṣaḍabhijño mahāvīro vajrasattvavināyakaḥ //	zaxaBijQaH mahAvIraH vajra sattva vinAyakaH //
   māradarpatamohantā saṃbodhijñānabhāskaraḥ /	mAra darpa tamaH hantA saMboDi jQAna BAskaraH /
   eṣa sa bhagavāṃlloke buddharatna iti smṛtaḥ //	eza sa BagavAn= loke budDa ratnaH iti smRtaH //
   (Gkv 4)	(Gku 4)
   ye caitaccharaṇaṃ gatvā boddhisattvā jagaddhite /	ye ca etat SaraNam gatvA bodDi sattvAH jagat hite /
   bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā caranto bhadracārikān //	boDi caryA vratam DRtvA carantaH BadracArikAn //
   jitvā māragaṇān sarvānarhanto nirmalāśayāḥ /	jitvA mAra gaNAn sarvAn arhantaH nirmala ASayAH /
   samyaksaṃbodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāgatāḥ //	samyaksaMboDim AsAdya saMbudDa padam AgatAH //
   te 'pi sarve jagannāthāstathāgatā munīśvarāḥ /	te api sarve jagannATAH taTAgatAH muni ISvarAH /
   bhagavanto mahābhijñā buddharatnā iti smṛtāḥ /	BagavantaH mahA aBijQAH budDa ratnAH iti smRtAH /
   yā śrī bhagavatī devī prajñā sarvaguṇāśrayā /	yA SrI BagavatI devI prajQA sarva guNa ASrayAH /
   jananī sarvabuddhānāṃ saṃbodhijñānabhāskarī //	jananI sarva budDAnAm saMboDi jQAna BAskarI //
   māradarpatamohantrī saddharmaguṇadāyinī /	mAra darpata maH hantrI sat Darma guNa dAyinI /
   sarvavidyādharī lakṣmī sarvasattvaśubhaṃkarī //	sarva vidyADarI lakzmI sarva sattva SuBaMkarI //
   eṣaḥ saddharmasambhartā dharmaratna iti smṛtaḥ //	ezaH sadDarma samBartA Darma ratnaH iti smRtaH //
   ye cānye 'pi mahāyānasūtrādayaḥ subhāṣitāḥ /	ye ca anye api mahAyAna sUtra AdayaH su BAzitAH /
   deśitāḥ sugataiste 'pi dharmaratna iti smṛtaḥ /	deSitAH sugatEH te api Darma ratnaH iti smRtaH /
   yaśca saddharmasaṃbhirtā bodhisattvo jagatprabhuḥ /	yaH ca sadDarma saMBirtA boDisattvaH jagatpraBuH /
   mahāsattvo jagannāthaḥ sarvadharmādhipeśvaraḥ //	mahAsattvaH jagannATaH sarva Darma aDipa ISvaraH //
   duṣṭakleśatamohantā saṃbodhigiṇabhāskaraḥ /	duzwa kleSa tamaH hantA saMboDi giNa BAskaraH /
   viśvarupo mahābhijñaḥ sarvasattvahitārthabhṛt //	viSvarupaH mahA aBijQaH sarva sattva hita arTa BRt //
   sarvalokādhipaḥ śrīmān dharmarājo jinātmajaḥ /	sarva loka aDipaH SrImAn DarmarAjaH jina AtmajaH /
   eṣa lokeśvaraḥ śāstā saṃgharatna iti smṛtaḥ //	eza loka ISvaraH SAstA saMGa ratnaH iti smRtaH //
   ye cānye 'pi mahāsattvā bodhisattvā jitendriyāḥ /	ye ca anye api mahAsattvAH boDisattvAH jita indriyAH /
   arhanto nirmalātmānaḥ saṃbodhijñānasādhinaḥ //	arhantaH nirmala AtmAnaH saMboDi jQAna sADinaH //
   bhadracaryāsamācārāścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ /	Badra caryA samAcArAH catur brahma vihAriNaH /
   saṃbuddhasāṃghikāste 'pi saṃgharatnāḥ smṛtā jinaiḥ //	saMbudDa sAMGikAH te api saMGa ratnAH smRtAH jinEH //
   ye teṣāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaktiśraddhāsamāhitāḥ /	ye tezAm SaraNam gatvA Bakti SradDA samAhitAH /
   bhajanti sarvadā nityaṃ smṛtvāpi ca divāniśam //	Bajanti sarvadA nityam smRtvA api ca divAniSam //
   te bhavanti mahāsattvā bodhisattvā guṇākarāḥ /	te Bavanti mahAsattvAH boDisattvAH guNa AkarAH /
   sacchrīsaṃpatsamāpannāḥ sarvasattvahitotsavāḥ //	sat SrI saMpad samApannAH sarva sattva hita utsavAH //
   bodhicaryāvrataṃ dṛtvā kṛtvā loke śubhaṃ sadā /	boDi caryA vratam dRtvA kRtvA loke SuBam sadA /
   sukhānyeva sadāa bhuktvāa prānte yāanti sukhāvatīm //	suKAni eva sadAa BuktvAa prAnte yAanti suKAvatIm //
   (Gkv 5)	(Gku 5)
   ityevaṃ saṃgharatnasya bhajanaṃ puṇyamuttamam /	iti evam saMGa ratnasya Bajanam puNyam uttamam /
   matvā taccharaṇaṃ gatvā bhajantyetadguṇārthinaḥ //	matvA tat SaraNam gatvA Bajanti etat guNa arTinaH //
   etatpuṇyaviśuddhātmā kadāpyeti na durgatim /	etat puNya viSudDa AtmA kadApyeti na durgatim /
   sarvadā sadgatiṣveva jāto dharmādhipo bhavet //	sarvadA sat gatizu eva jAtaH Darma aDipaH Bavet //
   ye cāpi dharmaratnasya pragatvā śaraṇaṃ sadā /	ye ca api Darma ratnasya pragatvA SaraNam sadA /
   bhajanti śraddhayā bhaktyā śrutvāpyetatsubhāṣitam //	Bajanti SradDayA BaktyA SrutvA api etat suBAzitam //
   te 'pi santo mahāsattvā bodhisattvā guṇāśrayāḥ /	te api santaH mahAsattvAH boDisattvAH guNa ASrayAH /
   saṃbodhiśrīsukhādhārāḥ sarvasattvaśubhāratāḥ //	saMboDi SrI suKa ADArAH sarva sattva SuBA ratAH //
   saṃbodhicārikāṃ dhṛtvā kṛtvā sattvahitaṃ sadā /	saMboDi cArikAm DRtvA kRtvA sattva hitam sadA /
   satsukhānyeva bhuktvānte saṃyānti sugatālayam //	sat suKAni eva BuktvA ante saMyAnti sugata Alayam //
   ityevaṃ dharmaratnasya bhajanārthaṃ varaṃ vṛṣam /	iti evam Darma ratnasya Bajana arTam varam vRzam /
   vijñāya śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajantvetacchubhārthinaḥ //	vijQAya SaraNam gatvA Bajantu etat SuBa arTinaH //
   etaddharmaviśuddhātmā durgatiṃ naiva yāti saḥ /	etad Darma viSudDa AtmA durgatim na eva yAti saH /
   sadgatiṣveva saṃjāto prāonte yāti jinālayam //	sat gatizu eva saMjAtaH prAonte yAti jina Alayam //
   iti vijñāya ye martyāḥ saddharmasukhavāṃchinaḥ /	iti vijQAya ye martyAH sadDarma suKavAMCinaH /
   triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajantu te sadā bhave //	tri ratna SaraNam gatvA Bajantu te sadA Bave //
   etatpuṇyānubhāvena pariśuddhāśayā narāḥ /	etat puNya anuBAvena pariSudDa ASayAH narAH /
   saṃbodhicittamāsādya caranti bodhisaṃvaram //	saMboDi cittam AsAdya caranti boDi saMvaram //
   bodhicaryāṃ carantaste pūrya pāramitāḥ kramāt //	boDi caryAm carantaH te pUrya pAramitAH kramAt //
   caturmārān vinirjitya niḥkleśā vimalāśayāḥ /	catur mArAn vinirjitya niHkleSAH vimala ASayAH /
   arhantaṃ prāpya saṃbodhiṃ saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ //	arhantam prApya saMboDim saMbudDa padam ApnuyuH //
   iti vijñāya yo martyaḥ saṃbuddhapadamicchati /	iti vijQAya yaH martyaH saMbudDa padam icCati /
   sa ādau śaraṇaṃ gatvā sadguroḥ samupāśrayet //	saH AdO SaraNam gatvA sat guroH samupASrayet //
   ārādhya sadguruṃ bhaktyā santoṣya saṃprasādayan /	ArADya sat gurum BaktyA santozya saMprasAdayan /
   tadupadeśamāsādya tīrtha snātvā vrataṃ caret //	tat upadeSam AsAdya tIrTa snAtvA vratam caret //
   vratānāṃ poṣadhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ samākhyātaṃ munīśvaraiḥ /	vratAnAm pozaDam SrezWam samAKyAtam muni ISvarEH /
   etatpuṇyānubhāvena saṃprāpnoti bodhimuttamām //	etat puNya anuBAvena saMprApnoti boDim uttamAm //
   atītā api saṃbuddhā etatpuṇyānubhāvataḥ /	atItAH api saMbudDAH etat puNya anuBAvataH /
   jitvā mārān samāsādya saṃbodhimabhavan jināḥ /	jitvA mArAn samAsAdya saMboDim aBavan jinAH /
   (Gkv 6)	(Gku 6)
   ye caitarhi sthitāḥ sarve te 'pyetatpuṇyabhāvataḥ /	ye ca etarhi sTitAH sarve te api etat puNya BAvataH /
   arhantaṃ prāpya saṃbodhiṃ bhavanti sugatāḥ khalu //	arhantam prApya saMboDim Bavanti sugatAH Kalu //
   ye cāpyanāgatāḥ sarve bodhisattvā vratopamāḥ /	ye ca api anAgatAH sarve boDisattvAH vrata upamAH /
   te 'pyetatpuṇyapākena bhaviṣyanti munīśvarāḥ //	te api etat puNya pAkena Bavizyanti muni ISvarAH //
   evamanyetatpuṇyapākena bhaviṣyanti munīśvarāḥ //	evam anyetat puNya pAkena Bavizyanti muni ISvarAH //
   evamanye 'pi sattvāśca ye ye 'pyetadvrataṃcarāḥ /	evam anye api sattvAH ca ye ye api etat vrataMcarAH /
   te te sarve mahāsattvā bhaveyurbodhibhāginaḥ //	te te sarve mahAsattvAH BaveyuH boDi BAginaH //
   śrīmantaḥ sadguṇādhārā niḥkleśā vijitendriyāḥ /	SrImantaH sat guNa ADArAH niHkleSAH vijita indriyAH /
   sarvasattvahitodyuktāścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ //	sarva sattva hita udyuktAH catur brahma vihAriNaH //
   durgatiṃ te na gacchanti kadāpi hi bhavālaye //	durgatim te na gacCanti kadApi hi Bava Alaye //
   sadāpi sadgatāveva saṃjātāḥ satsukhānvitāḥ /	sadA api sat gatO= eva saMjAtAH sat suKa anvitAH /
   bodhisattvāḥ sudhīmantaḥsaddharmaguṇasādhinaḥ //	boDisattvAH suDIm antar sad Darma guNa sADinaH //
   krameṇa bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā samāhitāḥ /	krameNa boDi saMBAram pUrayitvA samAhitAH /
   trividhāṃ bodhimāsādha nirvṛtipadamāpnuyuḥ //	triviDAm boDimAsADa nirvRti padam ApnuyuH //
   iti vijñāna ye martyā nirvṛtipadakāṃkṣiṇaḥ /	iti vijQAna ye martyAH nirvRti pada kAMkziNaH /
   te etad vratamādhāya saṃcaranto yathāvithi //	te etat vratam ADAya saMcarantaH yaTA viTi //
   etatpuṇyaviśuddhā hi naiva gacchanti durgatim /	etat puNya viSudDAH hi na eva gacCanti durgatim /
   sadā sadgatisaṃjātāḥ prānte yayuḥ sunirvṛtim //	sadA sat gati saMjAtAH prAnte yayuH su nirvRtim //
   evaṃ me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ munīndraideśitaṃ yathā /	evam me guruNA Adizwam muni indrEdeSitam yaTA /

   13. vārāṇasī kṛmi kīṭoddhāraṇa prakaraṇa	13. vArANasI kRmi kIwa udDAraNa prakaraNa

   20. phalaśrutiḥ	20. Pala SrutiH
   atha bhūyaḥ sa rājendro bhūpo 'śokaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ /	aTa BUyas sa rAja indraH BUpaH aSokaH kRtAMjaliH /
   upaguptaṃ tamarhantaṃ natvālokyedamabravīt //	upaguptam tam arhantam natvAlokya idam abravIt //
   bhadanta lokanātho 'sau yadāvalokiteśvaraḥ /	Badanta lokanATaH asO yadA avalokita ISvaraH /
   iti nāmnā prasiddho 'bhūttatkena samupādiśa //	iti nAmnA prasidDaH aBUt tat kena samupAdiSa //
   (Gkv 282)	(Gku 282)
   iti saṃprārthite rājñā yatiḥ so 'rhanmahāmatiḥ /	iti saMprArTite rAjQA yatiH saH arhat mahAmatiH /
   aśokaṃ taṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivamādiśat //	aSokam tam mahA rAjam samAlokya evam AdiSat //
   śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditam /	SRNu rAjan mahABAga yaTA me guruNA uditam /
   tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvānubodhito bhava //	taTA aham te pravakzyAmi SrutvA anuboDitaH Bava //
   ṣaḍgatisambhavā lokāstraidhātubhuvanāśritāḥ /	zaxgati samBavAH lokAH trEDAtu Buvana ASritAH /
   teṣāṃ ye duḥkhitā duṣṭāḥ kleśāgniparitāpitāḥ //	tezAm ye duHKitAH duzwAH kleSa agni paritApitAH //
   tān sarvān sa jagannāthaḥ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayat /	tAn sarvAn sa jagannATaH kRpA dRzwyA avalokayat /
   tenāvalokiteśākhyaḥ prasiddhastrijagatsvapi //	tena avalokita ISa AKyaH prasidDaH trijagatsu api //
   ye ye sattvā jagadbhartrā kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokitāḥ /	ye ye sattvAH jagat BartrA kRpA dRzwyA avalokitAH /
   te te sarve vikalmāṣā bhaveyurvimalāśayāḥ //	te te sarve vikalmAzAH BaveyuH vimala ASayAH //
   ye 'pyasya trijagacchāstuḥ śṛṇuyurnām sādaram /	ye api asya trijagat SAstuH SRNuyuH nAm sa Adaram /
   vimuktapātakāste syurniḥkleśā vimalendriyāḥ //	vimukta pAtakAH te syuH niHkleSAH vimala indriyAH //
   duḥkhāgnau patito yo 'pi smṛtvā lokeśvaraṃ bhajet /	duHKa agnO patitaH yaH api smRtvA lokeSvaram Bajet /
   tadā taṃ sa mahāsattvaḥ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayan //	tadA tam sa mahAsattvaH kRpA dRzwyA avalokayan //
   tadā sa sahasā tasmādduḥkhāgneḥ parimuktitaḥ /	tadA sa sahasA tasmAt duHKa agneH parimuktitaH /
   śuddhendriyo viśuddhātmā bhavet saṃbodhimānasaḥ //	SudDa indriyaH viSudDa AtmA Bavet saMboDi mAnasaH //
   yo nadyā prohyamāṇo 'pi krandellokeśvaraṃ smaran /	yaH nadyA prohyamANaH api krandet lokeSvaram smaran /
   tadā sa bodhisattvastaṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet //	tadA sa boDisattvaH tam kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet //
   tadā dadyānnadī tasya gādhaṃ santaraṇārthinaḥ /	tadA dadyAt nadI tasya gADam santaraNa arTinaH /
   tataḥ sa sahasottīrya smṛtvā dharmarato bhavet //	tatas sa sahasA uttIrya smRtvA Darma rataH Bavet //
   yadā ca vaṇijaḥ sārthā naukāruḍhā mahāmbudhau /	yadA ca vaNijaH sArTAH nOkAruXA mahA ambuDO /
   ratnārthino mahotsāhaiḥ saṃkrameyuryathākramam //	ratna arTinaH mahA utsAhEH saMkrameyuH yaTAkramam //
   tatra nauḥ kālikāvātaiḥ preryamāṇām vilolitā /	tatra nOH kAlikA vAtEH preryamANAm vilolitAH /
   tarasā rākṣasīdvīpasamīpaṃ samupācaret //	tarasA rAkzasI dvIpa samIpam samupAcaret //
   tadā teṣāṃ mahādhīraḥ smṛtvā lokeśvaraṃ namet /	tadA tezAm mahA DIraH smRtvA lokeSvaram namet /
   lokeśastānstadā sarvān kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayan //	lokeSaH tAnH tadA sarvAn kRpA dRzwyA avalokayan //
   tatastāḥ kālikā vātā na careyuḥ prasāditāḥ /	tatas tAH kAlikAH vAtAH na careyuH prasAditAH /
   tato nau savaṇiksārthā svasti ratnākaraṃ vrajet //	tatas nO sa vaNij sArTA svasti ratna Akaram vrajet //
   (Gkv 283)	(Gku 283)
   tatra te vaṇijaḥ sarve labdharatnāḥ pramoditāḥ /	tatra te vaNijaH sarve labDa ratnAH pramoditAH /
   svasti pratyāgatāḥ svasti samiyuḥ svapuraṃ laghu //	svasti pratyAgatAH svasti samiyuH sva puram laGu //
   yadi daivādvipattiḥ syāt sarvatīrthajalāśraye /	yadi dEvAt vipattiH syAt sarva tIrTa jala ASraye /
   mṛtāste śoṣitātmānaḥ saṃprayāyuḥ sukhāvatīm //	mRtAH te Sozita AtmAnaH saMprayAyuH suKAvatIm //
   yaśca duṣṭo vadhāt sṛṣṭo gṛhīto vadhyaghātakaiḥ /	yaH ca duzwaH vaDAt sRzwaH gRhItaH vaDya GAtakEH /
   bhīto lokeśvaraṃ smṛtvā dhyātvā nāmāpyudāharet //	BItaH lokeSvaram smRtvA DyAtvA nAma api udAharet //
   tadā lośeśvarastaṃ sa kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet /	tadA loSa ISvaraH tam sa kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet /
   tataste ghātakāḥ sarve taṃ hantuṃ nābhiśaknuyuḥ //	tatas te GAtakAH sarve tam hantum na aBiSaknuyuH //
   yadi vighātito daivāt tyaktvā pāpāśrayāṃ mṛtaḥ /	yadi viGAtitaH dEvAt tyaktvA pApa ASrayAm mRtaH /
   śuddhāśayo viśuddhātmā saṃprayāyāt sukhāvatīm //	SudDa ASayaH viSudDa AtmA saMprayAyAt suKAvatIm //
   sarve yakṣāśca gandharvāḥ kumbhāṇḍā rākṣasā api /	sarve yakzAH ca ganDarvAH kumBANxAH rAkzasAH api /
   kinnarā garuḍā nāgā bhūtāḥ pretāḥ piśācikāḥ //	kinnarAH garuxAH nAgAH BUtAH pretAH piSAcikAH //
   lokeśvarasya bhaktāraṃ dhyātāraṃ smṛtibhāvinam /	loka ISvarasya BaktAram DyAtAram smRti BAvinam /
   nāmoccāraṇakartāraṃ draṣṭumapi na śaknuyuḥ //	nAma uccAraNa kartAram drazwum api na SaknuyuH //
   yaścāpi nigaḍairbaddhā sthāpito bandhanālaye /	yaH ca api nigaxEH badDA sTApitaH banDana Alaye /
   smṛtvā lokeśvaraṃ dyātvā tiṣṭhennāmāpyudāharet //	smRtvA lokeSvaram dyAtvA tizWet nAma api udAharet //
   tatkṣaṇe lokanāthastaṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet /	tad kzaNe lokanATaH tam kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet /
   tadā sa bandhanānmukto dharmābhiratato bhavet //	tadA sa banDanAt muktaH Darma aBiratataH Bavet //
   yaścāraṇye gṛhe vāpi caurairdhūtairupadrute /	yaH ca araNye gRhe vA api cOrEH DUtEH upadrute /
   smṛtvā lokeśvaraṃ dhyātvā namennāmāpyudāharet //	smRtvA lokeSvaram DyAtvA namet nAma api udAharet //
   tatkṣaṇe lokanāthastaṃ kṛpādṛṭyāvalokayet /	tad kzaNe lokanATaH tam kRpA dRwyA avalokayet /
   tadā te dhūrtakāścaurāḥ sarve yāyuḥ parāṅmukhāḥ //	tadA te DUrtakAH cOrAH sarve yAyuH parAFmuKAH //
   yaśca rogī sadā duṣṭaḥ kuṣṭhavyādhyācitāśrayaḥ /	yaH ca rogI sadA duzwaH kuzWa vyADi Acita ASrayaH /
   smṛtvā lokeśvaraṃ dhyātvā namennāmāpyudāharet //	smRtvA lokeSvaram DyAtvA namet nAma api udAharet //
   tatkṣeṇe lokanāthastaṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet /	tad kzeNe lokanATaH tam kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet /
   tadā sa vyādhito mukto nīrogī puṣṭitendriyaḥ //	tadA sa vyADitaH muktaH nIrogI puzwita indriyaH //
   śuddhāśayo viśuddhātmā bhavet saṃbodhimānasaḥ /	SudDa ASayaH viSudDa AtmA Bavet saMboDi mAnasaH /
   yadi daivādvipattiḥ syāddhitvā duḥkhāśrayaṃ tanum /	yadi dEvAt vipattiH syAt hitvA duHKa ASrayam tanum /
   śuddhāśayo viśuddhātmā saṃprayāyāt sukhāvatīm //	SudDa ASayaH viSudDa AtmA saMprayAyAt suKAvatIm //
   (Gkv 284)	(Gku 284)
   yaśca daridrito duḥkhī dīno 'nātho durāśrayaḥ /	yaH ca daridritaH duHKI dInaH anATaH durASrayaH /
   smṛtvā lokeśvaraṃ dhyātvā namennāmāpyudāharet //	smRtvA lokeSvaram DyAtvA namet nAma api udAharet //
   tatkṣaṇe lokanāthastaṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet /	tad kzaNe lokanATaH tam kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet /
   tadā sa śrīguṇotpanno bhavet sāadhuḥ śubhendriyaḥ //	tadA sa SrI guNa utpannaH Bavet sAaDuH SuBa indriyaH //
   yaśca saṃgrāmamadhye 'pi śatrubhiḥ pariveṣṭita /	yaH ca saMgrAma maDye api SatruBiH parivezwitaH /
   smṛtvā lokādhipaṃ dhyātvā namennāmāpyudāaharet //	smRtvA loka aDipam DyAtvA namet nAma api udAa haret //
   tatkṣaṇe lokanāthastaṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet /	tad kzaNe lokanATaH tam kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet /
   tadā so 'rīnvinirjitya labdhvā ramejjayaśriyam //	tadA saH arIn vinirjitya labDvA ramet jaya Sriyam //
   yaścāpi dahyamāneṣu gṛhodyānāśrameṣvapi /	yaH ca api dahyamAnezu gRha udyAna ASramezu api /
   smṛtvā lokādhipaṃ dhyātvā nāma proccārayannamet //	smRtvA loka aDipam DyAtvA nAma proccArayat namet //
   tatkāle lokanāthastaṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet /	tad kAle lokanATaH tam kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet /
   tadā sa sahasā vahniskandhaḥ śāmyennirākulaḥ //	tadA sa sahasA vahni skanDaH SAmyet nirAkulaH //
   vivāde kalaye vāpi paribhūte 'pi durjanaiḥ /	vivAde kalaye vA api pariBUte api durjanEH /
   smṛtvā lokeśvaraṃ dhyātvā nāma proccārayannamet //	smRtvA lokeSvaram DyAtvA nAma proccArayat namet //
   tatkṣaṇe lokaśāstā taṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet /	tad kzaNe lokaSAstA tam kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet /
   tadā sa vijayan sarvān saṃsthāpayennije vaśe //	tadA sa vijayan sarvAn saMsTApayet nije vaSe //
   yaśca kleśāgnisaṃtapto vyākulendriyamānasaḥ /	yaH ca kleSa agni saMtaptaH vyAkula indriya mAnasaH /
   smṛtvā lokaprabhuṃ dhyātvā namennāmāpyudāharan //	smRtvA loka praBum DyAtvA namet nAma api udAharan //
   tatkṣaṇe taṃ mahāsattvo dayādṛṣtyāvalokayet /	tad kzaNe tam mahAsattvaH dayA dRztyA avalokayet /
   tadā niḥkleśabhadrātmā bhavedbhadrendriyaḥ sudhīḥ //	tadA niHkleSa Badra AtmA Bavet Badra indriyaH suDIH //
   yo 'putraḥ putraratnārthī taṃ lokeśaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ /	yaH aputraH putra ratna arTI tam lokeSam SaraNam gataH /
   smṛtvā dhyātvā yathāśakti bhajennāmānyudāharan //	smRtvA DyAtvA yaTASakti Bajet nAmAni udAharan //
   tadā sa trijagadbhartā kṛpādṛṣṭyāvalokayet /	tadA sa trijagat BartA kRpA dRzwyA avalokayet /
   dadyāttasmai putraratnaṃ mahāsattvaṃ jagatpriyam //	dadyAt tasmE putra ratnam mahAsattvam jagat priyam //
   sutārthine 'pi satputrīṃ ramākārāṃ śubhendriyām /	suta arTine api sat putrIm rama AkArAm SuBa indriyAm /
   sarvasattvapriyāṃ kāntāṃ sādhvīṃ dadyājjagatprabhuḥ //	sarva sattva priyAm kAntAm sADvIm dadyAt jagat praBuH //
   vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ dhanārthi labhate dhanam /	vidyA arTI laBate vidyAm Dana arTi laBate Danam /
   rājyārthī labhate rājyaṃ lokeśabhaktimānapi //	rAjya arTI laBate rAjyam lokeSa BaktimAn api //
   (Gkv 285)	(Gku 285)
   dravyārthī labhate dravyaṃ guṇārthī labhate guṇam /	dravya arTI laBate dravyam guNa arTI laBate guNam /
   bhogyārthī labhate bhojyaṃ gṛhārthī labhate gṛham //	Bogya arTI laBate Bojyam gRha arTI laBate gRham //
   evamanyāni vastūni sarvopakaraṇānyapi /	evam anyAni vastUni sarva upakaraNAni api /
   yathābhivāṃchitaṃ sarvaṃ labhellokeśabhaktimān //	yaTA aBivAMCitam sarvam laBet lokeSa BaktimAn //
   tenāsau trijagannātha āryāvalokiteśvaraḥ /	tena asO trijagannATa Arya avalokita ISvaraH /
   iti prakhyāpitaḥ sarvairdharmarājaimunīśvaraiḥ //	iti praKyApitaH sarvEH DarmarAjA emuni ISvarEH //
   evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyaṃ lokeśabhaktibhāvinām /	evam mahattaram puNyam lokeSa Bakti BAvinAm /
   aprameyamasaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbuddhapadasādhanam //	aprameyam asaMKyeyam saMbudDa pada sADanam //
   ityevaṃ sugataiḥ sarvaiḥ samādiṣṭaṃ samantataḥ /	iti evam sugatEH sarvEH samAdizwam samantataH /
   bodhisattvairmahābhijñaiḥ sarvaiścāpi praśaṃsyate //	boDisattvEH mahA aBijQEH sarvEH ca api praSaMsyate //
   iti matvā mahārāja lokanāthasya sarvadā /	iti matvA mahA rAja loka nATasya sarvadA /
   śaraṇe samupāśritya bhajasva śraddhayā mudā /	SaraNe samupASritya Bajasva SradDayA mudA /
   yasya lokeśvare bhaktistasya pāpaṃ na kiṃcana /	yasya lokeSvare BaktiH tasya pApam na kiMcana /
   duṣṭakleśabhayaṃ nāpi nirvighnaṃ satsukhaṃ sadā //	duzwa kleSa Bayam na api nirviGnam sat suKam sadA //
   sarve duṣṭagaṇā mārāḥ kṣīyante sarvataḥ sadā /	sarve duzwa gaNAH mArAH kzIyante sarvatas sadA /
   yamadūtādayaścāpi palāyeyuḥ parāṅmukhāḥ //	yama dUta AdayaH ca api palAyeyuH parAFmuKAH //
   lokeśabhktibhājāṃśca puṇyadhārā nirantarā /	lokeSa Bkti BAjAn= ca puNya DArA nirantarA /
   apreyā asaṃkhyeyāḥ pravardhante divāniśam //	apreyAH asaMKyeyAH pravarDante divAniSam //
   etatpuṇyānubhāvaistu saddharmastena labhyate /	etat puNya anuBAvEH tu sadDarmaH tena laByate /
   tatsaddharmānubhāvena saṃbuddho dṛśyate 'grataḥ //	tad sat Darma anuBAvena saMbudDaH dRSyate agratas //
   tato buddhānubhāvena bodhicittaṃ sulabhyate /	tatas budDa anuBAvena boDi cittam sulaByate /
   bodhipraṇidhicittena caryante bodhicārikāḥ //	boDi praNiDi cittena caryante boDi cArikAH //
   kramāt saṃbodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramam /	kramAt saMboDi saMBAram pUrayitvA yaTAkramam /
   sarvān kleśān vinirjityāacaturmāragaṇānapi //	sarvAn kleSAn vinirjityAa catur mAra gaNAn api //

   daśabhūmīśvaro bhūtvā saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyāt //	daSa BUmi ISvaraH BUtvA saMboDim samavApnuyAt //
   iti matvā mahābhijño lokeśvaro jinātmajaḥ /	iti matvA mahA aBijQaH loka ISvaraH jina AtmajaH /
   bhajanīyaḥ sadā sadbhiḥ saṃbuddhapadavāṃchibhiḥ //	BajanIyaH sadA sadBiH saMbudDa padava aMCiBiH //

   ye bhajanti sadā nityaṃ lokeśvaraṃ jagatprabhum /	ye Bajanti sadA nityam lokeSvaram jagatpraBum /
   teṣāṃ naiva bhayaṃ kiṃcitsarvatra sarvadāpi hi //	tezAm na eva Bayam kiMcid sarvatra sarvadA api hi //
   rakṣeyustaṃ samālokya brahyādayo maharṣayaḥ /	rakzeyuH tam samAlokya brahya AdayaH mahA RzayaH /

   dūrāddṛṣṭvābhirakṣeyustaṃ lokeśaśaraṇāśritam //	dUrAt dRzwvA aBiH akzeyuH tam lokeSa SaraNa ASritam //
   vajrapāṇyādayo vīrāḥ sarvamantrārthasādhakāḥ //	vajrapANi AdayaH vIrAH sarva mantra arTa sADakAH //
   rakṣeyustaṃ samālokya lokeśabhakticāriṇam //	rakzeyuH tam samAlokya lokeSa Bakti cAriNam //

   arhanto bhikṣavaścāpi dṛṣṭgā taṃ dūrato mudā /	arhantaH BikzavaH ca api dRzwgA tam dUratas mudA /
